***стена.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стена</a> (291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stěna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steyh₂-</i>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stone</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stain</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стена́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stená</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стены́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wall
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запереться.html>запере́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четырёх</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стена́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zaperétʹsja v četyrjóx <b>stenáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to immure oneself</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to lock up oneself up in four <b>walls</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:биться.html>би́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bítʹsja golovój ob <b>sténu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat one's head against the <b>wall</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:горох.html>горо́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak ob <b>sténu</b> goróx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">like talking to a stone <b>wall</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каменный.html>ка́менной</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стено́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak za kámennoj <b>stenój</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">safe</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">like a stone <b>wall</b></span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стенд.html>стенд</a> (9570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stand</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стенд.html>стенд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stɛnd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стенд.html>сте́нда</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стенд.html>сте́нды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стенд.html>сте́ндов</a></b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:степенный.html>степе́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stepénnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***степенный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:степенный.html>степе́нный</a> (30161)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stépenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with stress shift.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:степенный.html>степе́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stepénnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)степе́ннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)степе́нней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reasonable, solid, serious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:степенный.html>степе́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stepénnyj</b> čelovék</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reasonable/serious person</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:степенный.html>степе́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нрав.html>нрав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stepénnyj</b> nrav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reasonable/serious temperament</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>staid, sedate, grave
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:степенной.html>степе́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stepénnaja</b> žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">staid life</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:степенной.html>степе́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лица</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stepénnaja</b> úlica</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sedate street</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***степень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> (1084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stepenĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stǫpenь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступень.html>ступе́нь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stépenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пени</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пени</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>степене́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>degree, extent</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> power</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> degree of comparison</li>
<li>rank, title, degree
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ученый.html>учёная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">učónaja <b>stépenʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">scholastic degree</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мера.html>ме́ра</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">méra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступень.html>ступе́нь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stupénʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показатель.html>показа́тель</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pokazátelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***стерва.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стерва.html>сте́рва</a> (9993)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly from Old Russian, now obsolete <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стерво</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stervo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">carrion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. A similar word is Modern Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стервятник.html>стервя́тник</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stervjátnik</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vulture, carrion-eating bird</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стерва.html>сте́рва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stérva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стерва.html>сте́рвы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стерва.html>сте́рвы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стерва.html>сте́рв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bitch, vixen, old witch (a malicious, quarrelsome or temperamental woman)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bastard, son of a bitch, asshole (a malicious, quarrelsome or temperamental person)</li></ol>

***стервятник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стервятник.html>стервя́тник</a> (13294)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стерво</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stervo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">carrion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стервятник.html>стервя́тник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stervjátnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стервятник.html>стервя́тника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стервятник.html>стервя́тники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стервятник.html>стервя́тников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vulture</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стереть.html>стере́ть</a> (8913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стереться.html>стере́ться</a> (18746)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стереть.html>стере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sterétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стереться.html>стере́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sterétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стираться.html>стира́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be obliterated/effaced, to rub away, to become obliterated
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стереться.html>стере́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мяти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sterétʹsja</b> v pámjati</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be erased/effaced from memory</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надпись.html>на́дпись</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стереться.html>стёрлась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nádpisʹ <b>stjórlasʹ</b> ot vrémeni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the inscription has become obliterated by age</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стереть.html>стере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sterétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sterťi</i>, from earlier <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stergti</i>.

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*strьžьnь</i>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стержень.html>сте́ржень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stérženʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стержень.html>сте́ржня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стержень.html>сте́ржни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стержень.html>сте́ржней</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стержень.html>стержне́й</a></b>)
